mysql> -- fetch country names with population equal to any european country;
mysql> select name from country where population = any
    -> (select population from counrty where continent='european');
ERROR 1146 (42S02): Table 'world.counrty' doesn't exist
mysql> select name from country where population = any
    -> (select population from counrty where continent='Europe');
ERROR 1146 (42S02): Table 'world.counrty' doesn't exist
mysql> select name,population from country c1 where population = any
    -> (select population from country c2 where continent='europe' and c2.continent !=c1.continent);

| name                     | population |

mysql> -- fetch country with higest population
mysql> select name,population from country where population >=
    -> (select max(population) from country);

| name  | population |
+-------+------------+
| China | 1277558000 |
